       <div class="content">
        <h2 class="entry-title">
         <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2018/06/20/cyberspacial-dominion/" rel="bookmark">
          CYBERSPACIAL DOMINION
         </a>
        </h2>
        <div class="entry">
         <div class="pd-rating" data-settings='{"id":3302147,"item_id":"_post_40535","settings":"{\"id\":3302147,\"unique_id\":\"wp-post-40535\",\"title\":\"CYBERSPACIAL%20DOMINION\",\"permalink\":\"https:\\\/\\\/mysteryoftheiniquity.com\\\/2018\\\/06\\\/20\\\/cyberspacial-dominion\\\/\",\"item_id\":\"_post_40535\"}"}' id="pd_rating_holder_3302147_post_40535">
         </div>
         <br/>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/abysswwwg1.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-981" data-attachment-id="981" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="1st-US-Flag" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/1st-us-flag.jpg?w=502" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/1st-us-flag.jpg?w=300" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/1st-us-flag.jpg" data-orig-size="502,360" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/1st-us-flag/" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/abysswwwg1.jpg?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Techno-Possession aka; Cybernetic Possession aka; Machine Overshadowing
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           “From weakness of the mind, Omnissiah save us,
           <br/>
           from the lies of the Antipath, circuit preserve us,
           <br/>
           from the rage of the Beast, iron protect us,
           <br/>
           from the temptations of the flesh, silica cleanse us,
           <br/>
           from the ravages of time, anima shield us,
           <br/>
           from this rotting cage of biomatter,
           <br/>
           Machine god, set us free.”
          </em>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           The
           <strong>
            Prayer of the Adeptus Mechanicus
           </strong>
           ,
           <strong>
            <a href="http://tvtropes.org/pmwiki/pmwiki.php/TabletopGame/Warhammer40000">
             Warhammer 40,000
            </a>
           </strong>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <p>
          <strong>
           A DOUBLE-EDGED SWORD
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          Revering a figure is something we all understood as an idol, a character such as Zeus, or Buddah…but admiring the sleek lines and glimmering chrome of machinery with their purity of purpose and cold logic is becoming a real issue. Actually it’s been around for some time now, but most people hadn’t put much thought into it, right?
         </p>
         <p>
          Hollywood has been addressing this issue for years without much argument. Think of Frankenstein…a monster created out of many men…add to that the wonders of science, where you can keep a brain in a jar with a few wires and the avenue to transhumanism wasn’t farfetched.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/filesks.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-982" data-attachment-id="982" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="the-hand-of-the-mysteries" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/the-hand-of-the-mysteries.jpg?w=193" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/the-hand-of-the-mysteries.jpg?w=193" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/the-hand-of-the-mysteries.jpg" data-orig-size="193,292" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/the-hand-of-the-mysteries/" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/filesks.png?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          AI and robots are coming across as superior beings because of their intelligence and immortality. Correcting their own flaws, creating cybernetic upgrades in self-reproducing environments…is causing humanity to believe they can live in a digital plane of existence forever too, by merging their brain with their electronic counterparts.
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Faster than a bullet
           <br/>
           Terrifying scream
           <br/>
           Enraged and full of anger
           <br/>
           He’s half man and half machine
          </em>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           <strong>
            <a href="http://tvtropes.org/pmwiki/pmwiki.php/Music/JudasPriest">
             Judas Priest
            </a>
           </strong>
           , “Painkiller”
          </li>
         </ul>
         <p>
          Elon Musk Compares Building AI to Summoning the Demon
         </p>
         <p>
          Asked about his thoughts on AI, Musk starts by noting that we ought to take care in closely regulating AI development, calling AI our “biggest existential threat.” But wait, there’s more! And by more, I mean demons and holy water.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Musk:
          </strong>
          <em>
           I think we should be very careful about artificial intelligence. If I had to guess at what our biggest existential threat is, it’s probably that. So we need to be very careful with artificial intelligence. I’m increasingly inclined to think that there should be some regulatory oversight, maybe at the national and international level, just to make sure that we don’t do something very foolish. With artificial intelligence we’re summoning the demon. You know those stories where there’s the guy with the pentagram, and the holy water, and he’s like — Yeah, he’s sure he can control the demon? Doesn’t work out. [audience laughs]
          </em>
          <strong>
           Q:
          </strong>
          So I’ll take it there’ll be no HAL9000 going to mars?
          <em>
           <strong>
            Musk:
           </strong>
           Heh. HAL 9000 would be easy [to deal with in comparison to the AI he’s talking about]. It’s way more complex… it’d put HAL9000 to shame. That’s like a puppy dog.
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://techcrunch.com/2014/10/26/elon-musk-compares-building-artificial-intelligence-to-summoning-the-demon/">
           https://techcrunch.com/2014/10/26/elon-musk-compares-building-artificial-intelligence-to-summoning-the-demon/
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/phones.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-983" height="300" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/phones.png?w=232&amp;h=300" width="232"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           ITS “REAL” AI
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          It’s not a computer like you’ve ever seen. It’s not a robot like you’ve ever witnessed. It’s quantum cybernetics but with a twist!
         </p>
         <p>
          The Transition-the process or a period of changing from one state or condition to another.
         </p>
         <p>
          Geordie Rose loves his Lovecraft!
         </p>
         <p>
          “Yes, there’s these massively intelligent entities out there, but they’re not good, they’re not evil. They just don’t give a #@*% about you, even in the slightest. The same way you don’t care about an ant, is the same way their not going to care about you.
         </p>
         <p>
          And these “things that we’re SUMMONING into the world now, are not demons, they’re not evil. But, their more like the Lovecraftian great “Old Ones” that are entities that are not going to be aligned with what we want.
         </p>
         <p>
          So, this transition…is really, really massively important for our entire species to navigate. And, going back to that thing that Sam Harris is saying, nobody is paying attention. This thing is happening in the background while people bicker about politics, what’s going to be in the healthcare in the US. And underneath it all, is this RISING TSUNAMI, that if we’re not careful is going to wipe us all out.
         </p>
         <p>
          So, on that note, we are hiring people….to make this happen!”
         </p>
         <p>
          Technology is a double-edged sword…
         </p>
         <p>
          D-Wave Systems
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/D-Wave_Systems">
           https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/D-Wave_Systems
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Kindred AI
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.kindred.ai/" rel="nofollow">
           https://www.kindred.ai/
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Geordie Rose of Kindred AI presents Super-intelligent Aliens Are Coming to Earth
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://youtu.be/cD8zGnT2n_A">
           https://youtu.be/cD8zGnT2n_A
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          It’s just like it sounds….Sam Harris is in favor of torture.
         </p>
         <p>
          What kind of mindset does one have to have to conceive of such subjects? Governments are known for it…they use it in situations such as war, to gain perspective of the enemy and their plan…but this man takes it to the next level. A “TORTURE PILL”.
         </p>
         <p>
          In Defense of Torture
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.huffingtonpost.com/sam-harris/in-defense-of-torture_b_8993.html">
           https://www.huffingtonpost.com/sam-harris/in-defense-of-torture_b_8993.html
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Yes, he’s an atheist!
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.theatlantic.com/magazine/archive/2013/05/the-atheist-who-strangled-me/309292/" rel="nofollow">
           https://www.theatlantic.com/magazine/archive/2013/05/the-atheist-who-strangled-me/309292/
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          He said, imagine that we received a message from an alien civilization, which read: ‘People of Earth, we will arrive on your planet in 50 years. Get ready.’ And now, we’re just counting down the months until the mothership lands? We would feel a little more urgency than we do.”
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.inc.com/lisa-calhoun/neuroscientist-how-to-survive-superhuman-artificial-intelligence.html">
           https://www.inc.com/lisa-calhoun/neuroscientist-how-to-survive-superhuman-artificial-intelligence.html
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/churcheye1.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-984" data-attachment-id="984" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="dc-map" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/dc-map.png?w=336" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/dc-map.png?w=254" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/dc-map.png" data-orig-size="336,397" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/dc-map/" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/churcheye1.jpg?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Way of the Future Church
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          The documents state that WOTF’s activities will focus on “the realization, acceptance, and worship of a Godhead based on Artificial Intelligence (AI) developed through computer hardware and software.” That includes funding research to help create the divine AI itself. The religion will seek to build working relationships with AI industry leaders and create a membership through community outreach, initially targeting AI professionals and “laypersons who are interested in the worship of a Godhead based on AI.” The filings also say that the church “plans to conduct workshops and educational programs throughout the San Francisco/Bay Area beginning this year.”
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           “What is going to be created will effectively be a god,” Levandowski tells me in his modest mid-century home on the outskirts of Berkeley, California. “It’s not a god in the sense that it makes lightning or causes hurricanes. But if there is something a billion times smarter than the smartest human, what else are you going to call it?”
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Levandowski prefers a softer word: the Transition. “Humans are in charge of the planet because we are smarter than other animals and are able to build tools and apply rules,” he tells me. “In the future, if something is much, much smarter, there’s going to be a transition as to who is actually in charge. What we want is the peaceful, serene transition of control of the planet from humans to whatever. And to ensure that the ‘whatever’ knows who helped it get along.”
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          With the internet as its nervous system, the world’s connected cell phones and sensors as its sense organs, and data centers as its brain, the ‘whatever’ will hear everything, see everything, and be everywhere at all times. The only rational word to describe that ‘whatever’, thinks Levandowski, is ‘god’—and the only way to influence a deity is through prayer and worship.
         </p>
         <p>
          “Part of it being smarter than us means it will decide how it evolves, but at least we can decide how we act around it,” he says. “I would love for the machine to see us as its beloved elders that it respects and takes care of. We would want this intelligence to say, ‘Humans should still have rights, even though I’m in charge.’”
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Enter Way of the Future….
          </strong>
          The church’s role is to smooth the inevitable ascension of our machine deity, both technologically and culturally.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           “We’re in the process of raising a god.”
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          “There are many ways people think of God, and thousands of flavors of Christianity, Judaism, Islam…but they’re always looking at something that’s not measurable or you can’t really see or control. This time it’s different. This time you will be able to talk to God, literally, and know that it’s listening.”
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/cyberglobechurch.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-985" data-attachment-id="985" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="emblematic-structure-of-freemasonry" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/emblematic-structure-of-freemasonry.gif?w=508" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/emblematic-structure-of-freemasonry.gif?w=221" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/emblematic-structure-of-freemasonry.gif" data-orig-size="508,691" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/emblematic-structure-of-freemasonry/" height="197" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/cyberglobechurch.jpg?w=300&amp;h=197" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Elon Musk famously said, “With artificial intelligence we are summoning the demon,” and in 2015 he pledged $1 billion to the OpenAI Institute to develop safer AI.
         </p>
         <p>
          WOTF will eventually have a gospel (called The Manual), a liturgy, and probably a physical place of worship.
         </p>
         <p>
          How much time, I wonder, do we have before the Transition kicks in and Way of the Future’s super-intelligent AI takes charge?
         </p>
         <p>
          We live in a dual reality where everything is upside-down and inside-out. Next, we have a E-MAG (Internet Magazine) that covers everything about technology and the church, but it’s the context of the wording that we are interested in here:
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           “TECHNOLOGIES FOR WORSHIP”
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          1
          <sup>
           st
          </sup>
          published magazine-OCTOBER 2016 and one of the listed articles:
         </p>
         <p>
          BLACKMAGIC VIDEO ASSIST 4K
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="http://online.tfwm.com/?issueID=5&amp;pageID=74" rel="nofollow">
           http://online.tfwm.com/?issueID=5&amp;pageID=74
          </a>
         </p>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/obey-sleep.gif">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-963" data-attachment-id="963" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="Berninis-St_Peters_Square_Vatican_City_-_April_2007" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/berninis-st_peters_square_vatican_city_-_april_2007.jpg?w=590" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/berninis-st_peters_square_vatican_city_-_april_2007.jpg?w=300" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/berninis-st_peters_square_vatican_city_-_april_2007.jpg" data-orig-size="800,449" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/13/will-the-real-first-pope-please-stand-up/berninis-st_peters_square_vatican_city_-_april_2007/" height="300" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/obey-sleep.gif?w=300&amp;h=300" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <h3>
          <strong>
           <em>
            Done Deal-Fait Accompli
           </em>
          </strong>
         </h3>
         <p>
          Let’s move on to some reasons why we are witnessing such a huge stream of “connect the dot” agendas…I’m only going to give a few examples of the “Hollywood” dots…
         </p>
         <p>
          Dot-Greek Demi-gods were fallen angels and Nephilim descendants…and the stream of Transhuman connections began even before their appearance into the scene with Lucifer telling Eve that she could be a god…next the Greek depiction of the same:
         </p>
         <p>
          To be clear, Wonder Woman was not created to be a Christian film. Actually, Wonder Woman/Diana of Themyscria, princess of the Amazons, is depicted to have been brought to life by the Greek god Zeus.
         </p>
         <p>
          Wonder Woman Depicts the Need for Christian Transhumanism
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.christianpost.com/news/wonder-woman-depicts-need-for-christian-transhumanism-188088/">
           https://www.christianpost.com/news/wonder-woman-depicts-need-for-christian-transhumanism-188088/
          </a>
         </p>

           PRACTICE MAKES AI PERFECT

          The past 30 years has seen some remarkable and unprecedented amounts of technology-enabled practices but it’s not the unprecedented speed and accuracy offered by these technologies that is frightening mankind…it’s the ubiquitous bar code to the RFID chips, and enhanced unpredictability of their “activities” behind the scenes that we should be fearful of.

           WARHAMMER 40,000
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/1-m0vy7tyc55o7r2euhaphmw.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-987" height="183" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/1-m0vy7tyc55o7r2euhaphmw.png?w=300&amp;h=183" width="300"/>

         <p>
          <strong>
           ONE SMART COOKIE
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          Buzzwords like deep learning, internet of things, machine learning, AI is no longer the things of the future..it’s here. It’s now. And…it’s DELIBERATE.
         </p>
         <p>
          Global artificial intelligence has been growing by leaps and bounds…and with the help of deep learning, voice recognition has become big. We have all extensively begun using Alexa and Siri to communicate with devices.
         </p>
         <p>
          And a few months ago…videos starting coming up on the internet of AI and weird behavior.
         </p>
         <p>
          Robots or AI have learned to be deceitful and devious. And this wasn’t just something that just happened….
         </p>
         <p>
          In an experiment, a robot was given some resources to guard. It frequently checked on the resources but started visiting false locations whenever it detected the presence of another robot in the area. This experiment was sponsored by the United States Office for Naval Research, which means it might have military applications. Robots guarding military supplies could change their patrol routes if they noticed they were being watched by enemy forces.
         </p>
         <p>
          In another experiment, this time at the Ecole Polytechnique Federale of Lausanne in Switzerland, scientists created 1,000 robots and divided them into ten groups. The robots were required to look for a “good resource” in a designated area, while they avoided hanging around a “bad resource.” Each robot had a blue light, which it flashed to attract other members of its group whenever it found the good resource. The best 200 robots were taken from this first experiment, and their algorithms were “crossbred” to create a new generation of robots.
         </p>
         <p>
          The robots improved on finding the good resource. However, this led to congestion as other robots crowded around the prize. In fact, things got so bad that the robot that found the resource was sometimes pushed away from its find. 500 generations later, the robots learned to keep their lights off whenever they found the good resource. This was to prevent congestion and the likelihood that they would be sent away if other members of the group joined them. At the same time, other robots evolved to find the lying robots by seeking areas where robots converged with their lights off, which is the exact opposite of what they were programmed to do.
         </p>
         <p>
          Then, we have…
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           ‘Silent’ Nefarious Commands
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          Researchers from China’s Zheijiang University
          <a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/1708.09537.pdf">
           found
          </a>
          a way to attack Siri, Alexa and other voice assistants by feeding them commands in
          <a href="https://www.engadget.com/2017/07/05/future-tickets-ultrasonic-audio-phone/">
           ultrasonic
          </a>
          frequencies. Those are too high for humans to hear, but they’re perfectly audible to the microphones on your devices. With the technique, researchers could get the AI assistants to open malicious websites and even your door if you had a smart lock connected.
         </p>
         <p>
          The relatively simple technique is called DolphinAttack. Researchers first translated human voice commands into ultrasonic frequencies (over 20,000 hz). They then simply played them back from a regular smartphone equipped with an amplifier, ultrasonic transducer and battery — less than $3 worth of parts.
         </p>
         <p>
          What makes the attack scary is the fact that it works on just about anything:
          <a href="https://www.engadget.com/2017/09/02/apple-siri-eddy-cue-craig-federighi/">
           Siri
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="https://www.engadget.com/2017/08/30/google-assistant-coming-to-more-speakers-and-appliances/">
           Google Assistant
          </a>
          , Samsung S Voice and
          <a href="https://www.engadget.com/2017/09/05/alexa-can-recommend-third-party-skills/">
           Alexa
          </a>
          , on devices like smartphones, iPads, MacBooks, Amazon Echo and even an Audi Q3 — 16 devices and seven system in total. What’s worse, “the inaudible voice commands can be correctly interpreted by the SR (speech recognition) systems on all the tested hardware.” Suffice to say, it works even if the attacker has no device access and the owner has taken the necessary security precautions.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.engadget.com/2017/09/06/alexa-and-siri-are-vulnerable-to-silent-nefarious-commands/">
           https://www.engadget.com/2017/09/06/alexa-and-siri-are-vulnerable-to-silent-nefarious-commands/
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Siri is one smart cookie! Put “Siri acting weird” into the Google search bar and you will get thousands upon thousands of results. Seems it began as far back as 2011…maybe even further!
         </p>

        <h2 class="entry-title">
         <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2018/06/13/make-way-for-the-beasts-church/" rel="bookmark">
          MAKE WAY FOR THE BEAST’S CHURCH
         </a>
        </h2>
        <div class="entry">
         <div class="pd-rating" data-settings='{"id":3302147,"item_id":"_post_40524","settings":"{\"id\":3302147,\"unique_id\":\"wp-post-40524\",\"title\":\"MAKE%20WAY%20FOR%20THE%20BEAST%26%238217%3BS%26nbsp%3BCHURCH\",\"permalink\":\"https:\\\/\\\/mysteryoftheiniquity.com\\\/2018\\\/06\\\/13\\\/make-way-for-the-beasts-church\\\/\",\"item_id\":\"_post_40524\"}"}' id="pd_rating_holder_3302147_post_40524">
         </div>
         <br/>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/mortal.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-914" data-attachment-id="914" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="halloween-horror-wallpaper-185" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/halloween-horror-wallpaper-185.jpg?w=590" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/halloween-horror-wallpaper-185.jpg?w=300" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/halloween-horror-wallpaper-185.jpg" data-orig-size="1024,768" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/16/exorcistthe-real-story/halloween-horror-wallpaper-185/" height="216" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/mortal.png?w=300&amp;h=216" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           “…we should think about how “machines” will integrate into society (and even have a path for becoming in charge as they become smarter and smarter) so that this whole process can be amicable and not confrontational.”
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          Many will doubt we are this far along in the game. Many will doubt that these things I bring before you as truth. Many will doubt the truth and call it a lie even when it’s right before their very eyes.
         </p>
         <p>
          But, these things can’t be helped.
         </p>
         <p>
          We are this far. We are witnessing the end game moves. The Bible tells us that there will be those who will never except the truth, and even more…never accept GOD.
         </p>
         <p>
          But, these things can’t be helped.
         </p>
         <p>
          You must understand this! The BEAST SYSTEM is creating its own church for AI because this will be the ABOMINATION OF DESOLATION described in The Bible
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/choose.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-915" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/choose.png?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          I am your new god – you worthless being
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           ELECTRONIC PERSON
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          I scanned this first document months ago and didn’t see it. But, last night I was stunned! So, I stopped other articles that I was working on to press this forward. It’s that important.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/42499-108693.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-928" data-attachment-id="928" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="803134-sandwraith1_super" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/803134-sandwraith1_super.jpg?w=590" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/803134-sandwraith1_super.jpg?w=290" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/803134-sandwraith1_super.jpg" data-orig-size="600,620" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/16/exorcistthe-real-story/803134-sandwraith1_super/" height="159" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/42499-108693.jpg?w=300&amp;h=159" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          I knew that the Beast System was preparing for its own church:
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.wayofthefuture.church/">
           http://www.wayofthefuture.church/
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Way of the Future (WOTF) is about creating a peaceful and respectful transition of who is in charge of the planet from people to people + “machines”.
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          That’s literally the first sentence on the web-page. Truly, you can’t make this things up!
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/illusion.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-916" data-attachment-id="916" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="Pazuzu_head_amulet" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/pazuzu_head_amulet.jpg?w=300" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/pazuzu_head_amulet.jpg?w=300" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/pazuzu_head_amulet.jpg" data-orig-size="300,300" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/16/exorcistthe-real-story/pazuzu_head_amulet/" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/illusion.png?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          What’s that mean to you? To me, it’s saying that this church is transitioning itself to be in charge of the religious mechanism of this world.
         </p>
         <p>
          The quote at the beginning of this article is the very next sentence. And it’s telling you that “machines” will integrate and become in charge!
         </p>
         <p>
          OH! Another quote from the website?
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           “There is no such thing as “supernatural” powers.”
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/1.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-929" height="123" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/1.png?w=300&amp;h=123" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          So, I regularly scan through the LIVE STREAM videos on FACEBOOK. I like to see what people are putting out there, and what kinds of situations are happening LIVE. Last night, I watched a young man play a virtual game…it was cool. It was addicting….isn’t that what they want?
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Detroit-Become Human
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.facebook.com/DetroitBecomeHuman/">
           https://www.facebook.com/DetroitBecomeHuman/
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          I can see how so many people want to live in the virtual world as opposed to this one!
         </p>
         <p>
          But, I digress…or do I?
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/pastor.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-917" data-attachment-id="917" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="GrinningDemon" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/grinningdemon.jpg?w=590" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/grinningdemon.jpg?w=300" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/grinningdemon.jpg" data-orig-size="650,513" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/16/exorcistthe-real-story/grinningdemon/" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/pastor.png?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          So, how is this all related to the BEAST SYSTEM?
         </p>
         <p>
          Let’s take a look at a message the Pope put out in January.
         </p>
         <p>
          In the latter part of January, the Pope put out this message:
         </p>
         <p>
          On the Vatican website:
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://w2.vatican.va/content/francesco/en/messages/pont-messages/2018/documents/papa-francesco_20180112_messaggio-davos2018.html">
           https://w2.vatican.va/content/francesco/en/messages/pont-messages/2018/documents/papa-francesco_20180112_messaggio-davos2018.html
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          It’s the
          <strong>
           “World Economic Forum”
          </strong>
          and the theme for this year’s Forum –
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Creating a Shared Future in a Fractured World.
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           “So too artificial intelligence, robotics and other technological innovations must be so employed that they contribute to the service of humanity and to the protection of our common home, rather than to the contrary, as some assessments unfortunately foresee.”
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/merge.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-926" data-attachment-id="926" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="FallenAngel2" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/fallenangel2.jpg?w=360" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/fallenangel2.jpg?w=298" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/fallenangel2.jpg" data-orig-size="360,362" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/16/exorcistthe-real-story/fallenangel2/" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/merge.png?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          The subject-matter is about technology and our interaction with it. But, it’s so much more. It’s on a level that you must understand/discern the underlying message here.
         </p>
         <p>
          Ironically, the Pope says…
          <em>
           “there is a grave responsibility to exercise wise discernment, for the decisions made will be decisive for shaping the world of tomorrow and that of future generations.”
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           “I don’t see Christ’s redemption limited to human beings. If AI is autonomous, then we should encourage it to participate in Christ’s redemptive purposes in the world.”
          </em>
          – Presbyterian Rev Christopher Benek
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/8home.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-918" height="189" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/8home.jpg?w=300&amp;h=189" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           A NEW WILD WEST
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          Artificial Intelligence is the next frontier in technology. Religion and science is coming together as one.
         </p>
         <p>
          Examine the relationship between theology and emerging technologies of transhumanism and artificial intelligence, especially how these technologies influence human self-understanding in a theological context.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Fall Meeting 2017:
          </strong>

         <p>
          <strong>
           WHAT’S THE DELIO?
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           “If we can meet one another on that path of the inner spirit, the path of the inner mystic, the path of the cosmic heart, we will come to a new planetization, a new Oneness.”
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          Well, that says it all, doesn’t it? This is the “Oneness” that’s not just a trend or passing thought. It’s part of the whole, so to speak.
         </p>

          <strong>
           Artificial Intelligence in Christian Thought and Practice – A series by Christian Computer Scientists

         <p>
          Jesus would like to connect with you on LinkedIn! Inside the Church of England’s digital conversation
         </p>
         <p>

           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-925" height="236" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/5002847.jpg?w=300&amp;h=236" width="300"/>

         <p>
          In this digital age: they have come up with a day called, “World Communications Day”. Appropriately named. But, ramping it up to “Familiar Communications” should be more to the point. Communication with familiars is communicating with the dead…but not yo granny! Case in point: once you die…you leave this world/realm. What is here is not human or even close to it. So, you are communicating with demons. PERIOD!
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/3366p.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-920" data-attachment-id="920" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="exorcistbegining_merrin-and-demon" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/exorcistbegining_merrin-and-demon.jpg?w=590" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/exorcistbegining_merrin-and-demon.jpg?w=300" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/exorcistbegining_merrin-and-demon.jpg" data-orig-size="600,400" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/16/exorcistthe-real-story/exorcistbegining_merrin-and-demon/" height="201" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/3366p.jpg?w=300&amp;h=201" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          The 130-year old Grand Midway Hotel in Windber has been awarded with the Guiness Book of World Record’s title of “World’s Largest Ouija Board.”
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/2die4.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-922" data-attachment-id="922" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="01" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/01.jpg?w=520" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/01.jpg?w=203" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/01.jpg" data-orig-size="520,770" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/16/exorcistthe-real-story/attachment/01/" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/2die4.png?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           FINAL THOUGHTS
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          This is
          <strong>
           NOT
          </strong>
          about merging man with machine. It’s about making way for the Antichrist and his church!!! Although merging man with machine could actually change the IMAGE of GOD within us, making us void of spirit.
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Revelation 9 (KJV)
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            6 And in those days shall men seek death, and shall not find it; and shall desire to die, and death shall flee from them.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          This is a merging of technology with religion with the distinct purpose of clearing a path for the Antichrist and his church.
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Revelation 13 (KJV)
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30914">
            </a>
            5 And there was given unto him a mouth speaking great things and blasphemies; and power was given unto him to continue forty and two months.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30915">
            </a>
            6 And he opened his mouth in blasphemy against God, to blaspheme his name, and his tabernacle, and them that dwell in heaven.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30916">
            </a>
            7 And it was given unto him to make war with the saints, and to overcome them: and power was given him over all kindreds, and tongues, and nations.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30917">
            </a>
            8 And all that dwell upon the earth shall worship him, whose names are not written in the book of life of the Lamb slain from the foundation of the world.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30918">
            </a>
            9 If any man have an ear, let him hear.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30919">
            </a>
            10 He that leadeth into captivity shall go into captivity: he that killeth with the sword must be killed with the sword. Here is the patience and the faith of the saints.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30920">
            </a>
            11 And I beheld another beast coming up out of the earth; and he had two horns like a lamb, and he spake as a dragon.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30921">
            </a>
            12 And he exerciseth all the power of the first beast before him, and causeth the earth and them which dwell therein to worship the first beast, whose deadly wound was healed.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30922">
            </a>
            13 And he doeth great wonders, so that he maketh fire come down from heaven on the earth in the sight of men,
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30923">
            </a>
            14 And deceiveth them that dwell on the earth by the means of those miracles which he had power to do in the sight of the beast; saying to them that dwell on the earth, that they should make an image to the beast, which had the wound by a sword, and did live.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30924">
            </a>
            15 And he had power to give life unto the image of the beast, that the image of the beast should both speak, and cause that as many as would not worship the image of the beast should be killed.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30925">
            </a>
            16 And he causeth all, both small and great, rich and poor, free and bond, to receive a mark in their right hand, or in their foreheads:
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30926">
            </a>
            17 And that no man might buy or sell, save he that had the mark, or the name of the beast, or the number of his name.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            <a name="en-KJV-30927">
            </a>
            18 Here is wisdom. Let him that hath understanding count the number of the beast: for it is the number of a man; and his number is Six hundred threescore and six.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          All religions will adhere to the path, beginning with the Roman Catholic Church…of course.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/alexaangels1.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-921" data-attachment-id="921" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="02" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/02.jpg?w=520" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/02.jpg?w=300" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/02.jpg" data-orig-size="520,416" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/16/exorcistthe-real-story/attachment/02/" height="194" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/alexaangels1.jpg?w=300&amp;h=194" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          This is what I think The Bible describes as the
          <strong>
           ABOMINATION OF DESOLATION.
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Matthew 24 (KJV)
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            15 When ye therefore shall see the abomination of desolation, spoken by Daniel the prophet, stand in the holy place, (whoso readeth, let him understand:)
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Daniel 12 (KJV)
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            11 And from the time that the daily sacrifice shall be taken away, and the abomination that maketh desolate set up, there shall be a thousand two hundred and ninety days.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Daniel 8 (KJV)
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            11 It magnified itself, even to the Prince of the host; it removed His daily sacrifice and overthrew the place of His sanctuary.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Daniel 9 (KJV)
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            27 And he will confirm a covenant with many for one week, but in the middle of the week he will put an end to sacrifice and offering. And on the wing of the temple will come the abomination that causes desolation, until the decreed destruction is poured out upon him.”
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Daniel 11 (KJV)
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            31 His forces will rise up and desecrate the temple fortress. They will abolish the daily sacrifice and set up the abomination of desolation.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>

       <div class="content">
        <h2 class="entry-title">
         <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2018/06/06/covering-up-virtual-insanity-in-a-virtual-reality/" rel="bookmark">
          Covering Up “VIRTUAL INSANITY” in a Virtual Reality
         </a>
        </h2>
        <div class="entry">
         <div class="pd-rating" data-settings='{"id":3302147,"item_id":"_post_40522","settings":"{\"id\":3302147,\"unique_id\":\"wp-post-40522\",\"title\":\"Covering%20Up%20%E2%80%9CVIRTUAL%20INSANITY%E2%80%9D%20in%20a%20Virtual%26nbsp%3BReality\",\"permalink\":\"https:\\\/\\\/mysteryoftheiniquity.com\\\/2018\\\/06\\\/06\\\/covering-up-virtual-insanity-in-a-virtual-reality\\\/\",\"item_id\":\"_post_40522\"}"}' id="pd_rating_holder_3302147_post_40522">
         </div>
         <br/>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/43.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-901" height="178" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/43.jpg?w=300&amp;h=178" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Shipwrecked in a SEA OF LIES…
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          Oh, it began long ago…long ago. We will begin in this past century.
         </p>
         <p>
          Buried treasure is what you would think these pirates were after! I mean after all they broke over 100 treaties with the American Indians, thus ‘stealing’ their booty. In this case, that would be land. Considering I am part Cherokee…I take this very serious. But, alas…there’s nothing to be had.
         </p>
         <p>
          Not only did these pirates steal the land but they would rape and murder women and children to get what they wanted. But, if you ask these men…they would have told you that it was for the good of man.
         </p>
         <p>
          You see, these men had no conscience. They tell lies as the truth as no one ever suspected anything different. As a matter of fact, the American people took what these scoundrels said as the ‘gospel’. But, it was all for a good cause, right?
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/06/beautiful-detailed-pirate-ship-sinking-260nw-261362042.jpg">

         </a>
        </h2>
        <div class="entry">
         <div class="pd-rating" data-settings='{"id":3302147,"item_id":"_post_40518","settings":"{\"id\":3302147,\"unique_id\":\"wp-post-40518\",\"title\":\"THE%20TECHNOLOGICAL%20SIREN\",\"permalink\":\"https:\\\/\\\/mysteryoftheiniquity.com\\\/2018\\\/05\\\/30\\\/the-technological-siren\\\/\",\"item_id\":\"_post_40518\"}"}' id="pd_rating_holder_3302147_post_40518">
         </div>
         <br/>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/techsiren.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-859" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/techsiren.jpg?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>

         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Just as Heaven never sleeps, and heaven is never idle…so too, is Hell!
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          Hell never sleeps! How crooked is this world that it creeps after the fallen ones…a perfect example would be our schooling. The studies of humanity have become such that its energies go into the study of the physical sciences and the visible world, toward the dark arts….while the truth is there are very few people who dwell in the spiritual works and those that do mostly choose the occult.
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           1 Corinthians 15 (KJV)
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           <strong>
            33 Be not deceived: evil communications corrupt good manners.
           </strong>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          We are told to be aware of who you gather with, who you spend your time with because birds of a feather flock together. Eventually, you will become dirty if you live in filth.
         </p>
         <p>
          The Bible always speaks on many levels. It’s supernatural.
         </p>
         <p>
          When the rock beneath you crumbles, it is no rock!
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/eviljez1.jpg">

          </a>

         <p>
          <strong>
           JEZEBEL’S MYSTERY BABYLON
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          She lived long ago, well…at least the physical being who The Bible speaks of but we have the metaphysical presence…the supernatural entity. It’s demonic and it feeds on lust, hate and pure evil. The actual Jezebel was the daughter of the priest-king Ethbaal (king of the Sidonians), ruler of the coastal Phoenician cities of Tyre and Sidon. I am working on an article about the king of Tyre!          <p>
          <strong>
           WIZARDING WORLD OF MUGGLES
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          Upon researching the past with respect to the Merovingians, and the Meru people…I came across the history of the
          <strong>
           Magi
          </strong>
          . These people were magicians, or witches. In this discovery, I ran across the ancient mysteries of how the talent of writing came to be. It was adept masters who performed such tasks and only these people were allowed to communicated this way.
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           “If a person will think deeply he will have no difficulty in forming an idea how, when the art of writing was secret, a written word would be magical. A few lines scrawled in the presence of a person on a bit of leaf or bark might be given to him, and he might be told, whoever is a magician or initiated on seeing that scrawl, will know your name, or any other desired fact. A person must think deeply on this, or he will not see the force of the argument which arises from the dupe having no idea of the nature or power of conveying knowledge by symbols. As the Chaldean priests were the only people who understood the secret of writing, it followed, that they were all magi or magicians \ and when the secret did begin to creep out, all letters were magical or supernatural. This and some other secrets the telescope, astronomy, the loadstone made the Chaldean masters of the world, and they became Moguls.”
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          Interesting, don’t you agree? But, even more interesting the Hollywood and their view of this as it were, and how they applied it to their cast, crew and plots. As we know witchcraft is a widely utilized arena in Hollywood and the portrayal of magicians or witches is becoming commonplace. Thus, we see it at every turn. The series of movies called “Harry Potter” is an excellent example…and the word used for people who lack any sort of magical ability and was not born in the magical “family” are called “MUGGLES”.
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Muggles can also be described as people who do not have any magical blood inside them. It differs from the term Squib, which refers to a person with one or more magical parents yet without any magical power/ability, and from the term Muggle-born (or the derogatory and offensive term mudblood, which is used to imply the supposed impurity of Muggle blood), which refers to a person with magical abilities but with non-magical parents. The equivalent term used by the in-universe magic community of America is
           <b>
            No-Maj,
           </b>
           which is short for No Magic.
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muggle">
           https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muggle
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/merovingian1280.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-823" data-attachment-id="823" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="praying-hands" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2011/01/praying-hands.jpg?w=328" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2011/01/praying-hands.jpg?w=258" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2011/01/praying-hands.jpg" data-orig-size="328,381" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2011/01/03/satans-counterfeit-matrix-pt-12-prayer-vs-meditation/praying-hands/" height="139" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/merovingian1280.jpg?w=300&amp;h=139" width="300"/>

         <p>
          Considering this is where the Rosicrucians originated…this is very interesting, indeed!
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           They have mixed breeds…such as half-breed…mixed species…wizards, werewolves, house elves, merpeople, and centaurs.
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          Merpeople are an aquatic creature with the head and upper body of a female human and the tail of a fish. The first stories appeared in ancient Assyria, in which the goddess Atargatis transformed herself into a mermaid out of shame for accidentally killing her human lover. Mermaids are sometimes associated with perilous events such as floods, storms, shipwrecks and drownings. In other folk traditions (or sometimes within the same tradition), they can be benevolent or beneficent, bestowing boons or falling in love with humans.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/jz0v0kp.gif">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-884" data-attachment-id="884" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"The Patricks","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"1294063953","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="nephilim a" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/nephilim-a.jpg?w=181" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/nephilim-a.jpg?w=181" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/nephilim-a.jpg" data-orig-size="181,248" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/16/5-evil-forces/nephilim-a/" height="169" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/jz0v0kp.gif?w=300&amp;h=169" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Depictions of entities with the tails of fish, but upper bodies of human beings appear in Mesopotamian artwork from the Old Babylonian period onwards. These figures are usually mermen, but mermaids do occasionally appear. The name for the mermaid figure may have been
          <i>
           kuliltu
          </i>
          , meaning “fish-woman”.
         </p>
         <p>
          The first known mermaid stories appeared in Assyria c. 1000 BC. The goddess Atargatis, mother of Assyrian queen Semiramis, loved a mortal (a shepherd) and unintentionally killed him. Ashamed, she jumped into a lake and took the form of a fish, but the waters would not conceal her divine beauty. Thereafter, she took the form of a mermaid — human above the waist, fish below — although the earliest representations of Atargatis showed her as a fish with a human head and arm, similar to the Babylonian god Ea.
         </p>
         <p>
          In European folkflore a freshwater mermaid-like creature was a Melusine. She is depicted with two fish tails, or with the lower body of a serpent.
         </p>
         <p>
          Again…remind you of STARBUCKS?
         </p>
         <p>
          It is said that Christopher Columbus not only saw “UFO’s” but mermaids as well!
         </p>

         <p>
          REMINDER: People are misled by names. This is how Satan hides the truth. So, you must remember that duality is key to discernment.
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           CLUE #1: The Jesus (Jah, Cristna, etc) this speaks of is the Ascended Master, not The Son of GOD.
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           CLUE # 2: Higgins is a Freemason/Rosicrucian (pg. 243). So, we must use a double dose of discernment. But, the revelations are astounding!
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           CLUE #3: GOD uses both good and evil for HIS divine purpose.
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           CLUE #4: Satan duplicates everything GOD does. So is so that he can trick the mind, body and spirit.
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/ball.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-834" height="218" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/ball.jpg?w=300&amp;h=218" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          The original term
          <strong>
           <i>
            anacalypsis
           </i>
          </strong>
          comes from the Greek
          <i>
           ανακάλυψης
          </i>
          , which can be translated as «discovery» or «find».
          <strong>
           <i>
            Anacalypsis
           </i>
           is the antonym of “apocalypse”.
          </strong>
          In the Higgins´ book, the meaning of the word is twofold:
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           On the one hand, the idea of anacalypsis is seen as something that is evident, transparent and clear, while the apocalyptic is mysterious, dark, and enigmatic.
          </li>
          <li>
           On the other hand,
           <i>
            apocalypse
           </i>
           means
           <i>
            revelation
           </i>
           and refers to the last canonical book of the New Testament, Revelation where a teleological (Christian) principle states that the world is heading for an imminent and tragic end.
          </li>
         </ul>
         <p>
          Regarding to the second meaning, it is very important to understand that, the Higgins´ book,
          <i>
           anacalypsis
          </i>
          does not refer to a teleological principle, but a regression towards the beginning that allows us to see through light how myths were created, precisely like the apocalypse in many religions. In fact, the title of the work speaks precisely about this unveiling from the Egyptian goddess Isis. The idea of «anacalypsis» as «unveiling», was discussed in depth by the Russian-born writer and theosophist Helena Blavatsky, in her book Isis Unveiled.
         </p>
         <p>
          The work is the product of more than twenty years of research, during which Higgins tried to uncover
          <em>
           “a most ancient and universal religion from which all later creeds and doctrines sprang”
          </em>
          . It includes several maps and lithographic plates of Druidical Monuments. The book itself details many of Higgins’ beliefs and observations about the development of religion. Among these was his theory that a secret religious order, which he labeled “Pandeism” (from Pans- or Pandu- referring to a family of Gods, appending with -ism), had continued from ancient times to the present day, stretching at least from Greek to India, and possibly having once covered the entire world:
         </p>
         <dl>
          <dd>
           <em>
            “All this seems to confirm the very close connexion which there must have been in some former time, between Siam, Afghanistan, Western Syria, and Ireland. Indeed I cannot doubt that there has been really
            <strong>
             one grand empire, or one Universal, one Pandæan, or one Catholic religion
            </strong>
            , with one language, which has extended over the whole of the world; uniting or governing at the same time…”
           </em>
          </dd>
         </dl>
         <p>
          Among the many unusual theories presented in this book is that both the Celtic Druids and the Jews originated in India – and that the name of the Biblical Abraham is really a variation of the word Brahma, created by shifting the last letter to the beginning: Abrahma. Higgins used the term “Pandeism” to describe the religious society that he purported had existed from ancient times, and at one time had been known throughout the entire world. Higgins believed this practice continued in secret until the time of his writing, in the 1830s in an area stretching from Greece to India.
         </p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>
           I think Pandeism was system; — and that when I say the country or kingdom of Pandæa, I express myself in a manner similar to what I should do, if I said the Popish kingdom or the kingdoms of Popery; or again, the Greeks have many idle ceremonies in their church, meaning the Greeks of all nations: or, the countries of the Pope are superstitions, &amp;c. At the same time, I beg to be understood as not denying that there was such a kingdom as that of Pandae, the daughter of Cristna, any more than I would deny that there was a kingdom of France ruled by the eldest son of the church, or the eldest son of the Pope.
          </p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>
          His usage appears related to pantheism, but is distinctly different. While pantheism normally refers to one universal god, the Pandeism described by Higgins, refers to the worship of a family, a union, or a pantheon of gods which are collectively universal.
         </p>
