         <pre class="western">Satan's twin:
 I believe Paradise or Tartarus to be in Tartary, the farther side of Meru, the mount on the side of the North, 
 where the Gods assembled in judgment. Though the Europeans made it hot, I have little doubt that the natives of a 
 country under a tropical sun tnade their hell cold. The same reason in part caused the Hindoos to place the mount 
 Meru in a temperate climate, on, the sides of the North. 
 
 
 Mystic Meru. The north pole was the Linga, surrounded by seven dwips or zones rising one above another, and seven seas, 
 or rivers, or waters, and an outward one called Oceanus. In this Oceanus the whole floated. Thus the earth, mother 
 Eartha, became the Argha or lone, and Meru the pole, the Linga. 
 <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/meru.jpg"><img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-836" height="156" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/meru.jpg?w=300&amp;h=156" width="300"/></a>
 
 In all ancient towns, we find an elevated place in the nature of a mount, called by different names. All these 
 mounts were imitations of the Meru of India. In Greece this was called the Acropolis- place of the Area, Arca-polis; 
 in Rome, the Capitol. 
 The Capitolium of Rome will be said to have been so called from an imaginary likeness to the head of a man, 
 it being the highest part. This may be true, but it was called caput for another reason : it was van icon or 
 model of the Meru, which was itself an icon of the sun and planetary bodies — the sun, the visible sign or icon 
 of the protogonos or Rasit of Moses, Rachid of the Arabians, Apx'/ of Greece, Caput-olium of Latium, and the 
 Area of Jerusalem.
 
 Agreeably to the just opinion of the Hindoo Theologians, the Pyramid on the banks of the Euphrates, an artificial 
 mountain raised in a flat country where there are no natural mountains, was the first erected copy of the holy 
 mount Meru or Ararat.
 
 The Jews and Greeks soon forgot the original Meru, and gave that name to some favourite mountain of their own country: 
 the first to Sion or Moriah. The Greeks had their Olympus and Mount Ida, near which was the city of Ilium, Aileyam in 
 Sanscrit, from Ida, whose inhabitants were Meropes, from Merupa : being of divine origin, or descended from Meru.
 "Meru is Olympus, or Olympus is Meru. There are several Olympuses, but only one Meru, though several less sacred 
 mounts, called Splinters of Meru. 
 
 In most countries there was a sacred mount, an Olympus, an Athos, or Atlas, or Ida, in short, a Meru — and a sacred city. 
 In Egypt, Thebes was the city; and as they could not conveniently Tiave a mount, without, in fact, going out of the 
 valley of the Nile, they had a sacred island, and this was Phylae or Meroe. 
 
 It appears from Diodorus Sicuius, that the Babylon of Egypt was built on a hill, which was selected for the purpose — 
 Meru, I can scarcely doubt. That Meroe was a Meru receives strong confirmation from the fact, that its priests had the 
 same name, Gymnosophists, as the Indian priests of Buddha. 
 
 The Hindoo religion states Mount Merou to be the Garden of Eden or Paradise, out of which went four rivers. These rivers 
 are the Burramputer, or Brahmapouter, the son of Brahma; secondly, the Ganges, Ganga or river female or Goddess Ganges, 
 in fact, a generic name for sacred rivers; thirdly, the Indus, Sind, and; fourthly, the Oxus, Gihon, or Djihhoun. 
 <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/eyeshaveit1.png"><img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-837" data-attachment-id="837" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="worldinhishanda" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/12/worldinhishanda.jpg?w=480" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/12/worldinhishanda.jpg?w=289" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/12/worldinhishanda.jpg" data-orig-size="480,499" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/12/02/satans-counterfeit-matrix-2/worldinhishanda/" height="210" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/eyeshaveit1.png?w=300&amp;h=210" width="300"/></a>
 
 These rivers were also called Chaishu, Bhadra, Sita, and Ganga, in the Hindoo language; and the country between two 
 of the rivers was called a douab, from duo-aub, like Mesopotamia. In like manner the rivers Euphrates and Tigris 
 were supposed to flow from Ararat and Paradise; but still one of them was thought to be the river Ganges, which flowed 
 underground from India, and appeared at the foot of the Armenian mountains: and they formed, likewise, a Mesopotamia. 
 The Nile also was supposed to be the Euphrates, which, by an underground channel, was conveyed into Africa. In this way 
 is accounted for the apparent absurdity of the Nile being one of the rivers of Paradise. The Ganges was called Padus, 
 one of the names of Buddha, and the same as the Eridanus of Italy. Whether the Euphrates, or the Tigris, or the Nile, 
 was ever called Padus I do not know; but I do know that Buddha was the sun, and that two of those rivers, the Ganges 
 and Mr. Waddington has justly observed, that the accounts of the building of Meroe by Cambyses, as given by Strabo 
 and Diodorus, are not worth notice. 
 
 The following description of the city on Meru is given by the author of Nimrod, with a copy of his plan :" In the sides 
 of the north," that is, at the North Pole, " according to the fictions of Indian mythology, is the pure and holy land of 
 Ilavratta, and in the centre of that land stands Brahma-puri, the city of the gods, and in the centre of Brahma-puri rises 
 Mount Meru, their Olympus. The forms which have been the subject of our discussion have been curiously combined on this 
 occasion. The land of Ilavratta is a perfect circle, but the city Brahma-puri is a perfect square; and instead of right 
 concentric lines fencing in the central sanctuary, eight circular towers are placed round the wall."
 The author of Nimrod has shown that Babylon was built with the tower in the middle of it, square in imitation of Meru, 
 or the Indian city of their Ararat, surrounded by streets, making seven concentric squares of houses, and seven spaces, 
 and twenty-eight principal streets (like the seven lands and seas of Meru), and the eighth, the outward fosse or Oceanus. 
 He has shown that the tower was formed upon seven towers, one above another, exactly as the Indian priests taught or 
 imagined that the world -was formed of belts of land and sea, step above step to the Meru or North Pole, in the centre 
 and at the top. Here appearsto be a complete jumble of astronomy and mythology. The seven seas and mount of the North, 
 Isaiah's seat of the gods, were theological, the seven planets astrological, and concealed from the vulgar. 
 
 Nimrod has shown, I think, pretty clearly, that Meru was sur- rounded with its paradise. Now we have seen how closely 
 Bacchus was connected with Meru, or this place of Paradise. Diodorus says, that Semiramis made a Garden or at a place 
 in the mountains of Media, called Baghistan, or the place of Baghis. Sir W. Jones had no doubt that Baghis was Bacchus. 
 
 Ecbatana, or Egbatana, in like manner, was built in seven enclosures, one rising above the other; it was in the mountains 
 of Media, and was the summer residence of the kings of Persia, who resided in the winter at Susa, the city of Memnon, 
 who was supposed to have built it Susa means Lotus or Lily — the city of the Lotus. 
 
 On the island of Bali, a small appendage to Java, are the ruins of an ancient temple, in which the mount Meru is exactly 
 copied. It is a square stone building, consisting of seven ranges of wall, each range decreasing as you ascend, till the 
 building terminates in a kind of dome. It occupies the whole of a small hill, which is shaped to receive the walls and to 
 accommodate itself to the figure of the whole structure. It contains 310 images of Buddha yet entire. This temple is in the 
 district of Kodu. This Kodu is a corruption of lodu or loud. Of this more hereafter. The Pagoda of Vilnour has seven storeys. 
 <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/3o85xvoxmyokxmh0nq.gif"><img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-815" data-attachment-id="815" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="princeofdarknesssides" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/princeofdarknesssides.jpg?w=590" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/princeofdarknesssides.jpg?w=300" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/princeofdarknesssides.jpg" data-orig-size="955,700" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/20/none-shall-buy-or-sell-without-the-mark/princeofdarknesssides/" height="240" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/3o85xvoxmyokxmh0nq.gif?w=300&amp;h=240" width="300"/></a>
 
 From the supposition that Meru or Ararat stood in the middle of the garden of paradise, came the attachment of all religions 
 to groves or gardens. In imitation of this, the hanging gardens were built at Babylon : rising like the seats of the 
 Amphitheatre at Verona, one above another, but oblong, in imitation of the elliptic Meru. These raised-up or hanging gardens 
 round the temple of Belus no doubt were in analogical imitation of the seven belts of land lising above one another around 
 Meru, and of the mystic garden of Paradise. In imitation also of Babylon and Meru, the city of lona, or the Syrian Antioch, 
 was built on seven hills, and was likewise supplied with its sacred groves, called the gardens of Daphne, which were very 
 famous. The gardens of Adonis; at Byblos, in this country, were also very celebrated. Daphne was the name of the bay tree 
 (sacred to Apollo the HELLENistic deity), and of the tree of knowledge of the Sibyl. In or near most cities where the 
 adoration of the Magna Mater prevailed, these gardens are to be found. The celebrated garden of delight, or Paradise of 
 Daphne, planted by Seleucus at lona or Antioch, was placed on the site of a former one, which was said to have been planted 
 by Hercules. 
 
 If, as I think cannot be denied, I have proved or shall prove that one universal religion — that of Buddha or Cristna 
 - pervaded the whole of the old world, the conduct of Seleucus, as I shall presently show, in the building of his city of 
 Antioch on the ruins of the ancient lona, in imitation of Babylon, Egbatana, Aia-aia, Mount Meru, will sufficiently 
 demonstrate the reason why we meet with the several Babylons, Troys, Sions, namely, that it proceeded from a superstitious 
 imitation of the first sacred city. In the old Greek authors a city called Aia-aia is often named. This means Earth of 
 Earthy or Land of Lands, It is celebrated as the residence of king iEetes, of the Orphic Argonauts, and was also the island 
 of Circe and Aurora. It had its central tower, its seven or eight precincts, its garden or grove: but I suppose it is merely 
 mythological, and in reality never did exist. Its remains are nowhere to be found. 
 
 Of Troy not much, is known, except that it was placed on seven hills. Near it was the famous Mount Ida or Gargarus, with 
 its Buddhist Gilga, or stone circle, or of Homer, seen and described by Dr. Clarke, where the gods were accustomed to assemble 
 on the sides of the North, In my Essay on the Celtic Druids (Ch. VI. Sect. XXL), I have given a quotation, with a translation, 
 from Homer, where the chiefs are represented as assembling in counsel, on seats, each at his stone pillar, in a circle. It 
 is only fair to suppose that the circle of stones found on Gargarus, by Dr. Clarke, were the very stones alluded to by Homer, 
 for they exactly suit to the description; and, by this fact, afford a remarkable piece of circumstantial evidence, that the 
 poem is not entirely destitute of foundation. 
 
 Rome was built upon seven hills, with a capitol or acropolis, which was square, and in other respects was an exact imitation 
 of Babylon. It is worthy of observation that Constantinople also was built, by the Christian Constantine, upon seven hills. 
 These circumstances tend to show that one secret system was at the bottom of them all. The oriental trinity is found in each 
 of the cities in different ways; but, after the observations on the universal prevalence of the trinity which the reader has 
 already seen, it is unnecessary to add more here. The word Troia or Troy, the district in which the city of Ilion was placed, 
 I have before observed means in Greek and Hebrew, three places: or, in English, Tripoly, of which name we have several towns 
 now remaining. 
 
 <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/04/devil-worshipper-puppymill-recordings_1280x.jpg"><img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-741" height="165" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/04/devil-worshipper-puppymill-recordings_1280x.jpg?w=300&amp;h=165" width="300"/></a>
 We can with certainty trace back the history of the Greeks till we are lost in absolute barbarism; and in that state we find 
 them in possession of gods, of whose origin they know nothing, except that the priests in their temples tell them they have 
 learned from their predecessors that they are foreigners, and that they came from the East or the North-east — some say by 
 land, others by sea. In the earliest periods there were no idols attached to these temples, but in lieu thereof, a plain 
 upright obelisk or stone pillar, which was daily anointed with oil. The God or Gods had then no names. By degrees they got 
 idols, and gave them names which are universally acknowledged to have come from the East or Egypt We examine these temples 
 and Gods now, and we find the earliest ceremonies in a language unknown to the Greeks— the names of the Gods unintelligible, 
 in fact, also in an unknown tongue. But we find these ceremonies and these names intelligible in the Sanscrit, and the same 
 ceremonies and Gods now in existence in India, the histories of which all agree in saying, that they were sent in remote times 
 to the West. We find as soon as the Greeks became civilised, that their learned men travelled to the East for knowledge, and 
 that they brought back with them the identical philosophical doctrines taught in India from the most remote antiquity : the 
 Metempsychosis and the Trinity, for instance. We are, however, desired to beheve, that the whole or the most important of 
 these facts, gods, and doctrines, were learned by the people of the East from those of the West, among whom it is asserted 
 they arose hundreds of years after we know that they were taught by the travelling philosophers. Surely persons who tell us 
 to believe this must think us very credulous. Nimrod says, "The word Syrian is oftentimes confounded by the Greeks with 
 Assyrian, but it doth nevertheless denote a very different country, that between Euphrates and the Mediterranean, famous or 
 infamous for the Ionian or Hellenic worship, for the lewd groves of Daphne, the mysteries of Hermaphroditus, and the Dove 
 temples of Hierapolis and Ascalon, at which last Semiramis was fabled to have been born. This was mere fable, for it only 
 means that that was the country of the Dove. The Syrians at large bore the appellation of Ionians and Ionites. 
 
 Again, Nimrod says, “From the Semiramis or Dove, the heretical people got the denomination of Ionic, which, as a sectarian 
 name, may apply to them all; but, as a Gentile name, was particularly affected by certain of the Pelasgi or Graics. The name 
 lone was borne by the Syrian city which afterwards took the title of Antiochia, and which, with its Daphne, was a great type 
 of Babylon; and also by other places. When Alexander of Abonos Teichos sought to reanimate Paganism by a sham Avatar of Apollo 
 Python, in the form of a serpent which he called PAvk-Ov, he requested of the Emperor that the town might change its name to 
 lono-Polis. The name was evidently applicable, and to Babylon, which city was the lona vetus of Propertius." 
 <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/ark111.png"><img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-839" height="167" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/ark111.png?w=300&amp;h=167" width="300"/></a>
 
 After this, Nimrod endeavours to show that the Ionians were emigrants from Babylon; that Ionia, in Greece, was founded by 
 one Caunus son of Miletus, son of the second Minos ; that the capital of Attica was a type of Babylon, and that it adopted, 
 to an unusual extent, the legends as well of the Diluvian as of the Tauric age; that the Acropolis, with its olive, was the 
 Ark-tower, which, he says, is the meaning of Acro-polis, or Acra : to which purpose may be noticed the Smyrnean coin. All 
 this evidently alludes to the celebrated Yoni or Argha. The Acro- polis was the high-place or the Meru. Again; that not less 
 than seven cities had the name of Athena, who was no other than the female principle in her warlike form, springing from the 
 head of Jupiter Ammon,and supporting her own party with wisdom and power; that one city was the Minyeian Archomenus, whose 
 citizens manned the Argo; that the emigration of these colonies was the celebrated, and the age in which it happened and that 
 Homer was one of these, and thence called an Ionian; that there were other colonies besides the Ionians, one of which 
 "bore the name of Aiol or the whole earth" (the iEolians), and others again that of D'Ore or D'Aour (the Dorians); that the 
 Bacchic pomp, in the Eleusinian mysteries or singing the liicchus, which he explains as the mysteries of the son.
 
 As the Chaldaean priests were the only people who understood the secret of writing, it followed, that they were all magi or 
 magicians and when the secret did begin to creep out, all letters were magical or supernatural. This and some other secrets 
 the telescope, astronomy, the loadstone made the Chaldaean masters of the world, and they became Moguls. Mogul is but Al-Mag, 
 The Mage. On this account all the princes of India desire to be invested with the pallium by the old Mogul of Delhi, successor 
 of Gengis Khan, of Tartary, the last incarnation of divine Wisdom. The mythos at last always reverts to its birth-place, 
 Indian Tartary the Mount Solima, the snow-capped Meru, where the Gods sit on the sides of the North. How the Mogul comes to be 
 Lord Paramount the world.
 This MN or Menu was in a particular manner the symbol of mind. Minos or Menu or Numa was a wise lawgiver. The only animal in 
 the creation possessing mind, called man for this reason. Thus the wisdom of the Sun became Solomon. With reference to the 
 same mythos we have the Men-des or holy Goat, which is the same as the Sheep. With reference to the same, we have the fig-tree 
 called Lamed, the sacred tree of the Indians, which fructifies in its own peculiar manner something like the Lotus. We have 
 also Mount Meru, called by the Siamese Menu, or, at least, Maria called Mania, which, combined with the circumstances that we 
 have seen relating to mounts and meres of the Aja or Lamb and Goat, justify a suspicion that Meru was Menu. With reference to 
 this, the centre letter of the two Irish alphabets is in one called Moiria, and in the other Muin, substituting the N and R 
 for one another, but each the centre letter. I cannot help suspecting, that all our Meres and Marias were corruptions of Menus 
 or arose from them.</pre>

 The Cabalistic Jews often insert the jod or prefix it to words, as they say, for the sake of a mystery; but in reality for 
 the same reason that the Irish Bishop writes his name X Doyle. This practice admitted, I believe that C-ama was both Cupid 
 and Venus, Cama and Cama-deva, HDD kme, desiderare, amare, 1 and was in fact C or X-ama. Cuma was the same, as was also 
 Kumari or Komari on Cape Cornarin, near which ruled the Xamorin or Zamorin, or Semiramis. Was Comarin the Coma-Marina ? I 
 believe that Caesar was X-sesar Tzar, whence the female Tzarina. I believe that IIX0YS, is I-IX0TS: 666?
 
 (Referencing X CHI, etc is something I've already covered!
 CHI-XI-STIGMA - <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2013/09/12/chi-xi-stigma-2/">https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2013/09/12/chi-xi-stigma-2/</a>
 I also found how this is connected to SIRIUS, ISIS, and NIBIRU/PLANET X:Parasakti, Adisakti, Devaki, and Parakta, have all 
 the same meaning. Para or Ad, and Devaki, mean the Deity, and sakti aflame. These are also the same as Bavani and Mama-ja. 
 Sometimes Parasakti is masculine, sometimes feminine. Sakti is also the same as verbum and sapiential Chati, I am persuaded, 
 is the same as Sacti, or named, Sci-akham, the meaning of the Saca or Xaca, and that it means the Logos, the Sapientia,

         <p>
          Anacalypsis An Attempt To Draw Aside The Veil Of The Saitic Esis Vol II

         <p>
          Not many people know this but language/alphabets, etc have been highjacked! And manipulated by witchcraft.

         <p>
          Anacalypsis or An Inquiry into the origin of Languages, Nations, and Religions

         <p>
          <a href="http://bucurialuisatan.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/Godfrey-Higgins-Anacalypsis-vol.-2.pdf">

         <p>
          Thoth was the Egyptian god of wisdom, and was sometimes metaphorically called ‘The Serpent of Wisdom’. It is thought by some that Thoth and the Mayan god Kukulcan are actually the same entity…
         </p>
         <p>
          The Eye in the pyramid archetype actually may have originated with the Triple-Goddess symbolism associated with Sirius. Sirius was referred to by some ancient sects as ‘The Mother Star’…
         </p>
         <p>
          The Greek word for this Great Mother was either written as a single letter, Mu, or as two succeeding letters, MU MU. Mu Mu also denotes Light, which was said to emanate magnificently from SIRIUS (and it does, of course, in comparison to other stars besides the Sun). Of course this relates to Atlantis.
         </p>

          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/readyfinal.jpg">

         <p>
          Light was/is known as the Menstruum of the Red Dragon to alchemists and high-level Freemasons. This relates to the Isis myths.

          <em>
           Eye of Horus, deeply associated with ISIS, was one version of the Eye in the Triangle
          </em>

          </em>

          The Red Dragon is ISIS, Sirius, etc. Red as a color has also been associated with Sirius for thousands upon thousands of years because Sirius appears red when it is close to the horizon…

          Delphi means the navel, and that it was called the center and navel of the earth. In the temple was a stone pillar from which we see many places built as an example of this, such as Stonehedge…etc. This is the origin of obelisks.

           FACT:
          </strong>
          The occupiers of the lands of the priests, when the crosier divided from the sword, held of the God Phre (Sun), and thus were free- men or men of the God Free, and exempt from military service. Thus, probably, arose the words free and free-men. They were men or tenants of the God Liber of Liber-tas, or Liber-ty.

          All clergy, priests…etc originated with the Druids.

         <pre class="western"><strong>FACT:</strong> The first were Seculars the second the Regulars, the Moines or Monks or Book-men. The mannus was descriptive of the 
 order of Menu, or sacred or secret order from the secret writing. 
 The Soc and the Boc describe the division of the caste functionaries, and second those whence the functionaries were taken, 
 into first, Regulars, i. e. Boc- manni, initiati or ordered ; and second, Seculars, not regulated, not ordered. The word 
 initiated' marks the distinction. In order to separate and know themselves, they initiated or circumcised themselves : 
 this was the secret, i. e. sacred rite. Is not sacred, Soc or Sac-rid, to be-rid, quit of free from the rule of monks, 
 as well as free from the rule of military service.
 
 The Budh of Ireland was of the family of Saca-sa, or the bonus Saca. This is the Sacya, from whom the Buddha Muni of the 
 Hindoos was descended.
 
 The Sacse are called Sagaa, hence come sacrum, sacrificium, sacerdos. The Romans had a priest called Sagart, from the 
 word Sag. There could be no sacrifice without this officer. From this word Cleland says came the Sac-erdos.
 
 The Franks were first heard of on the Rhine as Ale-manni. The word Frank means free, and is probably a corruption of the 
 word Free Liberi Sacae. This is the origin of the word Franchise. From this root may come our word Freehold, that is, land 
 held of the God. Our Freeholds are all held of a superior in theory they all have suit and service to perform to the liege 
 Lord, Priest or King, whichever it may be ; that is, Khan or Pri-est, meaning the real priest, in the Siam language, Sion, 
 that is, Sun, means free. Zion?
 Franci and Saxons were the same.  Perhaps the Franks might be a tribe of the Sacae. Italy had its name from Vitulus a Bull, 
 and every one knows the story of its Saturnalia; it was the country of Saturn ; but the Saturnalia were festivals of Saca. 
 Shesach was the Scythian king, and that the followers of Saturn and the Pallestini were Saxons. When we recollect the 
 striking manner in which the Saturn-ja is found in North India.
 Monks ; they were the Manni Om, the first word in regimine. Whenever the word Mannus is found, it seems always to have a 
 relationto something mystical, to the secret or mysterious doctrines. 
 The truth is, they ordained one another or initiated their brethren on admission, after serving their noviciate. Ordination 
 is nothing but initiation into the mysteries. 
 Wherever a nomade tribe made a settlement, the mythos of their ancient country was established, and this is the reason 
 why we have so many Merus or Moriahs, Parnassuses, Olympuses, Acropolises, &amp;c. They were all Mounts of Meru in miniature 
 they might be all said to be microcosms of the great one of North India.
 Essenes in each case to have been the professors of the highest order of the Cabala.
 We find a mote, hill or Olympus in most old towns. A metaphor.
 <strong>FACT: FREEMASON:</strong> In India, every trade was a secret, and called by the word Ras, secret wisdom or knowledge. Trades in 
 general constituted one great ras or caste; each trade again a little subcaste ; it had its own Ras each Ras had a Pontifex. 
 Each trade or craft or caste admitted persons to its ras only on payment of a fine and serving an apprenticeship. Every trade, 
 as well as that of Mason, was a craft : thus we have our crafts. When a person was taught the craft, he was admitted to be 
 a liber or free or soc man, of that craft. Every man who dwelt in the town was not a freeman ; but those only who understood 
 the liber or craft. 
 Almost all churches was the work of monastic masons, built by and for Monks for the Regulars not the Seculars.
 The Rosicrucians of Germany are quite ignorant of their origin ; but, by tradition, they suppose themselves descendants of 
 the ancient Egyptians, Chaldaeans, Magi, and Gymnosophists, and this is probably true. They had the name of illuminati, 
 from their claiming to possess certain secret knowledge, and, from their secrecy, they were also called invisible brothers. 
 They use as a mark of distinction or monogram the three letters F. R. C., which probably mean Fratres Rosi Crucis. Luther 
 took for his coat of arms, a cross rising from a rose. They are said to hold that an universal spirit pervades all nature, 
 which they call Argheus. 
 Here is evidently the Indian Argha. Under an old Carthusian convert at Baden, is a very curious series of secret prisons ; 
 they are said, in the town, to have belonged to the Inquisition but I have not been able to discover that it was ever 
 established there. On this account, and for some other reasons, I am induced to suspect that they belonged to these invisible 
 brethren. The circumstances of the gradation of ranks, the initiation, and the head of the order in Persia being called the 
 Grandmaster, raisesa presumption that the Sophees were, in reality, the order of Masons. The most eminent of them are called 
 Sheik, which is said tomean reverend, and this has the same meaning as worshipful. They are said to maintain, that the 
 dissolution of bodies by the power of fire is the only way in which men can arrive at the first principles of things. Here 
 I think we may perceive the resolution or reabsorption of all emanations into the First Principle, the Spiritual Fire, the 
 To Ov. The word Ros is, in English, dew by means of the similarity of this word to the word Ras, or wisdom, they seem to have 
 deceived their enemies, and sent them upon a false search. But I think there is no doubt that along with other matters they 
 were also Alchemists. 
 There is scarcely one of our very ancient customs, when examined to the bottom, which has not marks of the rule of the priests. 
 Look at a coronation, in any of the ancient kingdoms. Every thing bespeaks the appointment by the priest of his Lieutenant 
 or Vicra, or Vicar, after he has undergone, or is samached, or anointed with oil, from the vessel called Ampulla. 
 (Am is OM, and pulla is wisdom the vessel of the wisdom of Om,)
 Every inquirer into our ancient histories has read of the Sea Kings, who invaded the northern parts of the island from 
 Sandinavia.
 These were the people who had the Sagas for their sacred books. How came they to be Sea Kings? Were they like the Royal 
 Shepherdsof Egypt all kings. The Sea Kings were the Sagara or Sea Kings of Rama, in the island of Ceylon. 
 The island of lona had its name of Columba, from ancestors of those sea kings. From a very close attention to the nature of 
 the ancient mythologies, all which are intimately connected with astronomy, they imagined that man had been created, and that 
 the arts and sciences had take their rise, not far from the Arctic Circle, where the earth had first cooled and that they 
 had extended southwards as it became by degrees more and more cold.

        <h2 class="entry-title">
         <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2018/05/23/pillars-of-sailors/" rel="bookmark">
          “Pillars of Sailors”
         </a>
        </h2>
        <div class="entry">
         <div class="pd-rating" data-settings='{"id":3302147,"item_id":"_post_40509","settings":"{\"id\":3302147,\"unique_id\":\"wp-post-40509\",\"title\":\"%26%238220%3BPillars%20of%20Sailors%26%238221%3B\",\"permalink\":\"https:\\\/\\\/mysteryoftheiniquity.com\\\/2018\\\/05\\\/23\\\/pillars-of-sailors\\\/\",\"item_id\":\"_post_40509\"}"}' id="pd_rating_holder_3302147_post_40509">
         </div>
         <br/>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/inferno22.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-814" data-attachment-id="814" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="7" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/7.jpg?w=320" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/7.jpg?w=300" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/7.jpg" data-orig-size="320,266" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/20/none-shall-buy-or-sell-without-the-mark/7-2/" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/inferno22.png?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Esoteric knowledge is the opposite of wisdom. Mankind has been fooled for thousands of years by secret societies. A closed society of members formed a system, and in this system was a numeral symbolic language. These numbers and symbols (including the alphabet) created a system which could be found all around the world. To keep this secret symbolic language alive,
          <strong>
           Druid
          </strong>
          erected cyclic temples, lingas, obelisks and pillars to express their worship of particular deities. These sites include Stonehedge, among others. These numbers and symbols described on these pillars revealed that these people had extensive astronomical knowledge. This is no accident.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/3o85xvoxmyokxmh0nq.gif">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-815" data-attachment-id="815" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="princeofdarknesssides" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/princeofdarknesssides.jpg?w=590" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/princeofdarknesssides.jpg?w=300" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/princeofdarknesssides.jpg" data-orig-size="955,700" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/20/none-shall-buy-or-sell-without-the-mark/princeofdarknesssides/" height="240" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/3o85xvoxmyokxmh0nq.gif?w=300&amp;h=240" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          A perfect example of this would be
          <strong>
           The Caaba
          </strong>
          ! The very word itself was a mystery, so let’s look at this first. The word Caaba derived from the last part of the word Mercavah or Mercaba (or Shekinah) from the noun Recab. If you ask the history of this word, Mercaba…some will tell you it means
          <em>
           ‘the heavenly chariot’
          </em>
          . It was known as the vehicle or conveyor of the secret of the
          <strong>
           Om
          </strong>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/seapillar1.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-853" data-attachment-id="853" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="popww_prince-thumb" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/popww_prince-thumb.png?w=200" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/popww_prince-thumb.png?w=195" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/popww_prince-thumb.png" data-orig-size="200,307" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/19/axis-of-evil-3/popww_prince-thumb/" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/seapillar1.png?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          All ancient texts have one thing in common…they all refer to the different sections aboard these ‘chariots’ as ‘the seven heavens’, or (in the Zohar) as the ‘seven spheres’. The Zohar (Bereshith to Lekh Lekha), is quite detailed in its description of this chariot. It even describes the propulsion system that empowered the Mercaba. The Saphira and The Lebanah, Ophanims, lofty column of light, Seraphims, Nogah, Hayoth.
         </p>
         <p>
          This extends to the modern description of the
          <strong>
           Ka’aba
          </strong>
          . It’s a stone set into the Kaaba’ wall by Muhammad in 605 AD. Muslims believe it was once a part of the stones of heaven. They believe its origin to be supernatural.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/den.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-817" height="175" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/den.png?w=300&amp;h=175" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          A Temple was the circle or wheel of the heavens. The Caaba, with its
          <strong>
           360 pillars
          </strong>
          around it, was the temple of Mohammed (like the temple of Solomon). All the oldest temples of Zoroaster and the Indians were caves, acknowledged to be in imitation of the vault/circle/wheel of heaven. The black stone inside the circle is still adored as the emblem of the generative principle. The Caaba is said to have been planned originally in heaven, after the pattern of heaven, the circle of the sphere.
         </p>
         <p>
          Pillars were a symbolic gesture of worship, but they were inclusive of secret, unspoken languages of figures of high-level status but eventually they fell into common use and came to be the alphabets we know now.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/obeliskss.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-818" data-attachment-id="818" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="PhoenixRising" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/phoenixrising.jpg?w=387" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/phoenixrising.jpg?w=194" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/phoenixrising.jpg" data-orig-size="387,600" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/19/axis-of-evil-3/phoenixrising/" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/obeliskss.png?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          The name Cernunnos occurs only on the “Pillar of the Boatmen” (Pilier des nautes), which is a distinctive pillar stone. Divine representations liken it to the Celtic “horned god” with latter attributes of ruling over hidden treasures of the underworld…a chthonic (subterranean) dwelling, treasure guarding serpent that encircled the waist of the one it chose to protect. These legends associated it among the Cthulhu mythos, and the Olympian deities.
         </p>
         <p>
          The original pillar was a type of limestone which contained 4 tiers. The top depicts Cernunnos, Smertrios, and Castor and Pollux. The second tier, is Juptier, Esus, Tarvos Trigaranos and Vulcan.
         </p>
         <p>
          Esus is portrayed cutting branches from trees (Tree of Life?) with his axe. This is depicted as the
          <em>
           Divine Woodman hews the Tree of the Bull with Three Cranes
          </em>
          . Some think this is some allusion to events in the Cúchulainn saga. Rumors have it that he was a Celtic Jehovah.
         </p>
         <p>
          This is yet another twisting of Jesus Christ!
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/181cf2q.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-821" height="179" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/181cf2q.jpg?w=300&amp;h=179" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          People must see that the deities names change but the demon remains the same.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/f72cb096a2044f90bdc3e6032f035989.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-820" height="300" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/f72cb096a2044f90bdc3e6032f035989.jpg?w=243&amp;h=300" width="243"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          The
          <strong>
           Cú Chulainn
          </strong>
          , also spelled
          <strong>
           Cú Chulaind
          </strong>
          or
          <strong>
           Cúchulainn
          </strong>
          or
          <strong>
           Cuhullin
          </strong>
          is an Irish hero believed to be an incarnation of the god Lugh. This all shows striking similarities to the legends of Heracules. These legends are of the Ulstermen hunting a flock of magical birds overtaken by a snowstorm and seek shelter in a nearby house. Their host is Lug, a member of the supernatural race, Tuatha De Danann. Some believe them to be connected to the Tribe of Dan. From research I’ve gathered this is the same bloodlines as the Merovingians.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/merovingian1280.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-823" data-attachment-id="823" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="praying-hands" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2011/01/praying-hands.jpg?w=328" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2011/01/praying-hands.jpg?w=258" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2011/01/praying-hands.jpg" data-orig-size="328,381" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2011/01/03/satans-counterfeit-matrix-pt-12-prayer-vs-meditation/praying-hands/" height="139" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/merovingian1280.jpg?w=300&amp;h=139" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Merovingians are the offspring of the tribe of Dan which intermarried with the Canaanite Tuatha De Danann:
         </p>
         <p>
          All In The Dragon Family-
          <a href="https://watch.pairsite.com/dragon-lineage.html" rel="nofollow">
           https://watch.pairsite.com/dragon-lineage.html
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/now33.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-854" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/now33.png?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          “For as Abdul writes of The Necronomicon ‘civilizations were destroyed because of the knowledge contained in this book.’
          <strong>
           This is the deed that must be avenged
          </strong>
          , the memory of which slumbers in the blood of their human offspring – just as they slumber beneath the Earth, waiting for the day that the stars will be right again, and their descendants will
          <strong>
           perform the rites which will bring them up from the depths to reclaim their kingdom
          </strong>
          , and the Age of the Gods will begin anew: The New Atlantis, the New Jerusalem, the New World Order.” (“Dead But Dreaming: The Great Old Ones of Lovecraftian Legend Reinterpreted as Sumerian/Atlantean Kings”)
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/inferno3.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-819" data-attachment-id="819" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="earthheart1" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/12/earthheart1.jpg?w=361" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/12/earthheart1.jpg?w=298" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/12/earthheart1.jpg" data-orig-size="361,364" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/12/02/satans-counterfeit-matrix-pt2/earthheart1/" height="259" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/inferno3.png?w=300&amp;h=259" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          News:
         </p>
         <p>
          CERN’s New Particle Accelerator Is Ready to Launch
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           CERN, the top physics lab in the EU, has completed Linac 4, the new accelerator for use with the Large Hadron Collider.
          </li>
          <li>
           It will be in use by 2021, and may help scientists unlock the
           <strong>
            secrets of extra dimensions, dark matter, and dark energy
           </strong>
           .
          </li>
         </ul>
         <p>
          <a href="https://futurism.com/cerns-new-particle-accelerator-is-ready-to-launch/">
           https://futurism.com/cerns-new-particle-accelerator-is-ready-to-launch/
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/pillairs13.png">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-855" data-attachment-id="855" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="CTD_main_banner" data-large-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/ctd_main_banner1.jpg?w=530" data-medium-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/ctd_main_banner1.jpg?w=300" data-orig-file="https://mysteryoftheinquity.files.wordpress.com/2010/11/ctd_main_banner1.jpg" data-orig-size="530,243" data-permalink="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.com/2010/11/19/193/ctd_main_banner-4/" height="219" src="https://mysteryoftheiniquity.files.wordpress.com/2018/05/pillairs13.png?w=300&amp;h=219" width="300"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Pillar of the Boatmen
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pillar_of_the_Boatmen">

          FINAL THOUGHTS

          This is a connection to the pieces of the puzzle that is the web of chaos which Satan spreads. Some believe that using this giant machine to open portals…is the keys to the abyss.
